Service: The staff member Xiao Lin contacted me the day before arrival to inquire about room requirements and arrival time, and answered all my questions. The hotel staff were enthusiastic and their service made me feel at home. From the front desk to the room service, everyone had smiles on their faces. The service was attentive and any problems were solved perfectly after calling the front desk.
Hygiene: The room is clean and spacious, with complete hotel supplies and sufficient hot water for washing. The room service staff cleans carefully and the bedding and toiletries are replaced the next day.
Catering: The hotel also provides a rich buffet breakfast and various leisure facilities, and also experienced the ordering service delivered to the room, which is great
Environment and location: Very close to Jinan Olympic Sports Center. It takes less than ten minutes to walk slowly. There is a parking lot downstairs. It is about 25 minutes' drive from Jinan East Railway Station. You can also get there by subway.
All in all, this hotel is great. They also prepared a support package. Haha, it is very warm and left a deep impression on me. If I come to Jinan again, I will choose this hotel again.
